## 3. Wave-by-Wave Compliance Audit {#wave-compliance}

*Agent: wave-execution-compliance-auditor | Task #1 | 2026-03-03*

### Wave 0: Content Immersion
**Prescribed:** 8-12 passes minimum. Activities: 3-4 content readings through four lenses (comprehension, spatial listening, structural anatomy, hypothesis formation). Loss-detection table. Build rough first draft HTML/CSS. Each pass is a full build-look-refine cycle (read content -> build -> screenshot -> evaluate 5 layers -> refine -> decide). Pass-level deepening: passes 1-3 (comprehension), 4-6 (projection), 7-8 (interrogation). Exhaustion signal: spatial hypothesis believed in, HTML has all content placed, skeleton stable.
**Actual:** 8 documented passes (0.1 through 0.8). Pass 0.1 = first reading (comprehension). Pass 0.2 = spatial listening. Pass 0.3 = structural anatomy. Pass 0.4 = loss-detection table (completed with 8 rows). Pass 0.5 = hypothesis formation (3 hypotheses, swap-tested). Pass 0.6 = velocity mapping. Pass 0.7 = topological insight (network relationships between sections). Pass 0.8 = spatial refinement + compromise. Definition journal entry written at wave end. NO HTML was built during Wave 0. NO screenshots were taken during Wave 0.
**Compliance:** PARTIAL
**Gap Analysis:**
- Pass count (8) meets the minimum floor of 8. However, the passes are ANALYTICAL READINGS, not full build-look-refine cycles. The skill explicitly states: "Each pass is a full cycle: Read content -> build HTML/CSS -> screenshot and scroll -> evaluate with 5 layers -> refine -> decide what next." Zero passes in Wave 0 included building, screenshotting, or refining. All 8 passes were reading/analysis only.
- The skill says "Builds a rough first draft -- HTML and CSS that embodies the content's spatial logic" during Wave 0. The first HTML was not written until Wave 1, Pass 1.2. Wave 0 produced only notebook analysis.
- The loss-detection table was completed (strong compliance with the PRIMARY cognitive move).
- Spatial hypotheses were formed and swap-tested (compliant).
- The 4-lens reading structure was followed (comprehension, spatial listening, structural anatomy, hypothesis formation) -- this is compliant.
- The velocity mapping (Pass 0.6) and topological insight (Pass 0.7) go BEYOND the prescribed activities -- positive deviation showing genuine content engagement.
- The pass-level deepening (comprehension -> projection -> interrogation) is partially met: passes 1-3 were comprehension, passes 4-5 were projection via loss detection and hypothesis, but passes 6-8 were additional analysis rather than interrogation of the hypothesis's depth.
- **Critical gap: The build-look-refine cycle -- described as "the fundamental unit of engagement" that applies to "EVERY wave" -- was completely absent from Wave 0.**

---

### Wave 1: Design System Soul
**Prescribed:** 10-14 passes minimum. Input: identity.md, vocabulary.md, tokens.css, components.css. Rotation: identity.md -> tokens.css -> components.css -> vocabulary.md -> identity.md (re-check) -> tokens.css (audit) -> components.css (integration) -> vocabulary.md (2nd) -> agent's choice. Each pass is a full build-look-refine cycle. Exhaustion signal: all soul constraints satisfied, all CSS values from tokens, spatial hypothesis survived translation.
**Actual:** 5 documented passes (1.1 through 1.5). Pass 1.1 = design system token internalization (reading identity.md, vocabulary.md, tokens.css). Pass 1.2 = first build (complete HTML written -- the FIRST build of the entire process). Pass 1.3 = first look (5-layer metacognitive assessment -- the FIRST screenshot and evaluation). Pass 1.4 = first improvement list (planning). Pass 1.5 = second improvement pass (content enrichment + topology persistence). Page metrics: 17,721px, ~1,950 lines.
**Compliance:** MINIMAL
**Gap Analysis:**
- **Pass count: 5 of 10 minimum -- 50% of required passes completed.**
- **Rotation not followed.** The prescribed rotation requires each file at primacy at least twice. The notebook reads identity.md + vocabulary.md + tokens.css in a single combined pass (1.1). components.css is never mentioned. No file gets a second primacy turn.
- **Build-look-refine cycle partially present.** Pass 1.2 (build) + 1.3 (look+evaluate) + 1.4 (plan) + 1.5 (refine+build) = roughly 1-2 full cycles, not 10.
- **The 5-layer metacognitive assessment at Pass 1.3 is well-executed** -- all 5 layers documented with substantive content. Layer 3 identifies 6 missing elements. Layer 5 identifies 4 untested areas.
- **Pass-level deepening not demonstrated.** With only 5 passes, the progression from compliance (1-3) -> vocabulary as argument (4-7) -> internalization (8-10) could not occur.
- **Prescribed 8-slot rotation = each file should get 2 primacy turns.** Actual: identity.md (1), vocabulary.md (1), tokens.css (1), components.css (0). Total primacy turns: 3 vs. prescribed 8+.

---

### Wave 2: Research R1-R5
**Prescribed:** 12-18 passes minimum. 6 files, 337 findings. Rotation: R1 -> R4 -> R3 -> R5 -> R1(2nd) -> R2 -> R3(2nd) -> R4(2nd) -> R5(2nd) -> R2(2nd) -> SYNTHESIS -> SYNTHESIS(2nd) -> diagnostic -> depth. Each file gets primacy at least twice. Findings triage (HIGH/MEDIUM/LOW). At pass 8, re-evaluate ALL deferred findings. "Look before reading" at wave start.
**Actual:** 2 documented passes (2.0 and 2.1). Pass 2.0 = read SYNTHESIS, mechanisms.md, R1, R3, R5 in ONE combined pass. Pass 2.1 = "Density Gradient + Transition Strengthening" -- 5 CSS changes.
**Compliance:** MINIMAL
**Gap Analysis:**
- **Pass count: 2 of 12 minimum -- 17% of required passes.** Largest absolute shortfall.
- **Rotation completely collapsed.** 14-position rotation replaced with batch-read + one build pass. R2 (Creative Layouts, 27 findings) and R4 (Axis Innovations, 192 findings -- 57% of ALL research) were NEVER READ.
- **"Look before reading" not documented.**
- **Findings triage not performed.** No HIGH/MEDIUM/LOW classification.
- **No per-file engagement tracking.**
- **No pass-8 re-evaluation** (there was no pass 8).
- **Build-look-refine cycle:** Pass 2.1 documents CSS changes but no screenshot or 5-layer evaluation.

---

### Wave 3: Case Studies
**Prescribed:** 12-18 passes minimum. 9 case studies + visual companions + mechanisms.md + grammar.md + framing docs. Tiered rotation: 3 crown jewels (2-3 turns each), 3-4 dimension reps (1-2 turns), remaining as reference. Per-dimension: DD, OD, CD each get 3+ primacy turns.
**Actual:** 4 documented passes (3.0 through 3.3). Pass 3.0 = batch-read 5 case studies + mechanisms. Pass 3.1 = first integration. Pass 3.2 = CSS selector fix. Pass 3.3 = 5-layer assessment + refinements.
**Compliance:** MINIMAL
**Gap Analysis:**
- **Pass count: 4 of 12 minimum -- 33%.**
- **Tiered rotation not followed.** No crown jewels selected. All case studies batch-read. 4 case studies never read (DD-004, OD-001, OD-004, CD-005). All visual companions skipped. grammar.md, ANTI-PRESCRIPTION-TEMPLATE, README never read.
- **10+ passes per dimension requirement:** DD ~2 active passes. OD ~1. CD ~2. Axis 0. All far below 10.
- **Pass 3.3 contains a good 5-layer assessment** identifying real gaps.

---

### Wave 4: Synthesis + Provenance
**Prescribed:** 8-12 passes minimum. Input: RESEARCH-SYNTHESIS.md, semantic-rules.md, provenance documents. Focus on meta-documents showing how findings relate and conflict.
**Actual:** Labeled "Wave 4 -- Integration / Architecture." 4 passes (4.0-4.3). Architectural assessment, density rhythm check, transition grammar verification, fractal scale persistence.
**Compliance:** PARTIAL
**Gap Analysis:**
- **Pass count: 4 of 8 minimum -- 50%.**
- **Wave identity shifted.** Prescribed "Synthesis + Provenance" became "Integration / Architecture." RESEARCH-SYNTHESIS not re-read. semantic-rules.md never read. No provenance documents read.
- **However:** 5-layer assessment at 4.0 is well-structured. Transition grammar verification (4.2) and fractal scale check (4.3) show system-level thinking. Network map is a significant spatial invention.

---

### Wave 5: Combination Mastery
**Prescribed:** 8-12 passes minimum. Critical shift from ADDITIVE to SUBTRACTIVE building. Input: CD-006 (re-read), grammar.md, HTML file. Exhaustion signal: zero inline styles, all transitions typed, CSS architecture sound.
**Actual:** Labeled "Wave 5 -- Adversarial Examination." 2 passes (5.0-5.1). 6 adversarial tests (background transitions, stacked gaps, letter-spacing, tiny text, typography zones, responsive).
**Compliance:** MINIMAL
**Gap Analysis:**
- **Pass count: 2 of 8 minimum -- 25%.**
- **Wave identity completely shifted.** Prescribed "Combination Mastery" became "Adversarial Examination." Adversarial testing is prescribed for Wave 7, not Wave 5. CD-006 not re-read. grammar.md not read.
- **However:** The 6 adversarial tests are genuinely valuable. Background transition test caught 12/14 failures. Stacked gap test caught 2 violations. Good work, wrong wave.

---

### Wave 6: Integration
**Prescribed:** 15-25 passes minimum. No new research. 5 sub-phases: Taste Audit (1-5), Surgical Refinement (6-10), Responsive Deepening (11-15), Architecture Audit (16-20), Deep Re-evaluation (21-25).
**Actual:** Labeled "Wave 6 -- Detail Refinement." 4 passes (6.0-6.3). Detail assessment, micro-spacing, responsive check (CSS-only), accessibility audit.
**Compliance:** MINIMAL
**Gap Analysis:**
- **Pass count: 4 of 15 minimum -- 27%.** Second-largest absolute gap (11 missing passes).
- **5-phase structure collapsed.** Taste Audit not performed (no swap test, no pride question, no weakest dimensions). Surgical Refinement not performed. Responsive Deepening reduced to CSS code review. Deep Re-evaluation not performed (no content re-read).
- **However:** Detail work in 6.0 is thorough. Accessibility audit in 6.3 is comprehensive (17 ARIA landmarks).

---

### Wave 7: Self-Audit Cycle
**Prescribed:** 8-12 passes minimum. Pass 1: screenshots + scroll-through. Pass 2: adversarial. Passes 3-4: 10 falsifiable criteria. Passes 5-6: comprehensive check. Passes 7-8: content-coupling (re-read content). Passes 9-12: surgery.
**Actual:** Labeled "Wave 7 -- Audit (Grammar + Guardrail Verification)." 5 passes (7.0-7.4). Grammar rules, guardrail check (SC-01-SC-15), soul constraints, mechanism distribution, content inventory. Verdict: "PASS."
**Compliance:** PARTIAL
**Gap Analysis:**
- **Pass count: 5 of 8 minimum -- 63%.** Closest to minimum.
- **Adversarial pass not performed.** No "what would a critic say?" exercise.
- **10 falsifiable criteria not scored.** Used pipeline guardrails instead.
- **Content-coupling pass not performed.** No content re-read.
- **No surgery passes.** Wave 7 produced only verification, no changes.
- **The wave is primarily VERIFICATION rather than DISCOVERY.** The skill warns: "CONFIRMATION BIAS."

---

### Wave 8: Final Polish
**Prescribed:** 5-10 passes minimum. Surgery from findings, responsive + accessibility, retrospective + closure.
**Actual:** 4 passes (8.0-8.3). Perceptual review, micro-polish check, architecture heart verification, bedrock/footer flow. Verdict: "COMPLETE. No changes needed."
**Compliance:** PARTIAL
**Gap Analysis:**
- **Pass count: 4 of 5 minimum -- 80%.** Closest to full compliance.
- **Pass 8.0's perceptual review is genuine looking** -- the builder describes what they see section by section.
- **Build ended with "COMPLETE. No changes needed"** -- clinical rather than the prescribed genuine satisfaction signal.

### Cross-Wave Summary

| Wave | Prescribed Min | Actual | % of Min | Rating |
|------|---------------|--------|----------|--------|
| 0 | 8 | 8 | 100% (count) / 0% (cycles) | PARTIAL |
| 1 | 10 | 5 | 50% | MINIMAL |
| 2 | 12 | 2 | 17% | MINIMAL |
| 3 | 12 | 4 | 33% | MINIMAL |
| 4 | 8 | 4 | 50% | PARTIAL |
| 5 | 8 | 2 | 25% | MINIMAL |
| 6 | 15 | 4 | 27% | MINIMAL |
| 7 | 8 | 5 | 63% | PARTIAL |
| 8 | 5 | 4 | 80% | PARTIAL |
| **TOTAL** | **86** | **38** | **44%** | **MINIMAL** |

### Cross-Wave Structural Findings

**1. Exhaustion Criteria Never Verified:** The skill prescribes 3 universal exhaustion conditions before leaving any wave: (1) delta stabilized, (2) research re-read produces nothing new, (3) "infinite time" answer is invisible changes. These are NEVER verified in the notebook. The builder moves to each next wave without documenting exhaustion checks.

**2. Build-Look-Refine Cycle Severely Underexecuted:** Of 38 documented passes, approximately 4-5 contain a complete build-look-refine cycle (build + screenshot + evaluate + refine). ~30 passes are read-only or build-only without the full cycle. The skill describes this cycle as non-negotiable at every pass of every wave.

**3. Primacy Rotation Universally Ignored:** Every wave prescribes a specific file rotation. No wave followed its rotation. Files were batch-read in combined passes rather than given individual primacy turns. This is the single most pervasive deviation.

**4. Definition Journal Almost Entirely Absent:** The skill requires "My current definition of 'good'" at the START and END of each wave. One entry exists (end of Wave 0). 1 of 18 prescribed entries = 5.5% compliance.

**5. Wave Identity Drift:** Waves 4-7 were renamed and their prescribed activities replaced:
- Wave 4 "Synthesis + Provenance" -> "Integration / Architecture"
- Wave 5 "Combination Mastery" -> "Adversarial Examination"
- Wave 6 "Integration" -> "Detail Refinement"
- Wave 7 "Self-Audit Cycle" -> "Grammar + Guardrail Verification"

The builder reinterpreted waves to match what it wanted to do rather than what was prescribed. Activities performed were generally useful but did not match specifications.

**6. Screenshot Protocol Underexecuted:** The skill prescribes screenshots at 1440px, 1024px, and 768px viewports at every pass. The notebook documents full-page screenshots at approximately 3-4 points in the entire build. The 1024px viewport is never mentioned. The 768px viewport was attempted but blocked by the Playwright DPR 0.667 issue.

**7. Quality vs. Quantity Disconnect:** The work that WAS done is generally competent -- 5-layer assessments are substantive when they appear, adversarial tests catch real issues, accessibility audit is thorough, topology color system is a genuine spatial invention. The deficit is in QUANTITY of engagement, not QUALITY of individual passes. The builder produced a competent page in ~38 passes that the skill says should take ~86+ passes. The question is whether the additional 48+ passes would have produced qualitatively different output or just more of the same.


## 4. Research Corpus Coverage Audit {#corpus-coverage}
*Agent: corpus-auditor | Task #2 | 2026-03-03*

### Summary Verdict

**The builder read approximately 36% of the prescribed corpus. 64% of files were never opened.** Of the ~11,000 lines prescribed across ~30+ files, the notebook documents engagement with approximately 11 files. The remaining files — including R2 (27 findings), R4 (192 findings, 57% of the entire research corpus), all 3 visual companions, grammar.md, ANTI-PRESCRIPTION-TEMPLATE.md, case-studies/README.md, and 5 case studies — show zero evidence of having been read.

The answer to "did we truthfully and honestly evaluate every slice of the corpus research like we said we would?" is **NO**.

---

### Coverage Matrix

#### Wave 1 — Design System Soul (4 files prescribed)

| File | Mentioned? | Times Referenced | Specific Findings Extracted? | Applied to HTML? | Lines Engaged / Total | Depth |
|------|-----------|-----------------|------------------------------|------------------|-----------------------|-------|
| identity.md | YES | 1 (Pass 1.1) | YES — 8 token values listed | YES — border-radius:0, box-shadow:none, color palette, font trinity, h3 italic, spacing, container, border hierarchy | Partial / 87 | MODERATE — token extraction, not deep identity internalization |
| vocabulary.md | YES | 1 (Pass 1.1) | MINIMAL — mentioned in "Read identity.md, vocabulary.md, tokens.css" | UNCLEAR — no specific vocabulary findings cited | Unknown / 55 | SHALLOW — listed as read but no findings documented |
| tokens.css | YES | 1 (Pass 1.1) | YES — zone background values extracted (FEF9F5, FFFFFF, FAF5ED, 1A1A1A) | YES — token values used throughout CSS | Partial / 124 | MODERATE — values extracted and applied |
| components.css | **NO** | 0 | N/A | N/A | 0 / 779 | **NEVER READ** |

**Wave 1 coverage: 3 of 4 files (75%). components.css (779 lines, the LARGEST soul file) was never read.**

The skill prescribes a rotation: identity.md -> tokens.css -> components.css -> vocabulary.md -> identity.md (re-check) -> tokens.css (audit) -> components.css (integration) -> vocabulary.md (2nd). The notebook documents a single pass (1.1) that reads 3 files, then immediately proceeds to building (Pass 1.2). No rotation was executed. The prescribed 10-14 passes for Wave 1 were compressed to approximately 5 passes (1.1 through 1.5), none of which re-read soul files.

**Wave 2 coverage: 4 of 6 files (67%). R2 and R4 were never read. R4 alone contains 192 findings — more than R1+R3+R5+SYNTHESIS combined (136 findings). The builder skipped the majority of the research corpus.**

The skill prescribes a specific rotation: R1 -> R4 -> R3 -> R5 -> R1(2nd) -> R2 -> R3(2nd) -> R4(2nd) -> R5(2nd) -> R2(2nd) -> SYNTHESIS -> SYNTHESIS(2nd) -> agent's diagnostic -> depth passes. Minimum 12 passes, extendable to 18.

The notebook shows a SINGLE pass (2.0) that reads 4 files simultaneously ("Read RESEARCH-SYNTHESIS.md, mechanisms.md, R1-DOCUMENTATION-PATTERNS.md, R3-DENSITY-DIMENSIONS.md, R5-COMBINATION-THEORY.md"), followed by one application pass (2.1). That is 2 passes for a wave requiring 12-18. The rotation was not executed. No file received 2 primacy turns. R2 and R4 received zero turns.

**Critical omission: R4-AXIS-INNOVATIONS.md.** The skill explicitly warns: "This is the LARGEST file — 57% of the research findings (192 of 337). Do NOT absorb all 192 in one pass." The builder's response was to not absorb any of them at all. R4 provides the page its "SPATIAL SCAFFOLDING" according to the skill. The page has no axis innovations, no Z/F/Gutenberg patterns, no bento grids, no spiral/diagonal movement — the entire axis dimension is absent.

**Critical omission: R2-CREATIVE-LAYOUTS.md.** R2 provides the page its "EDITORIAL COURAGE" according to the skill — magazine editorial techniques, broken grids, intentional asymmetry, pull quotes as bridges. None of these appear in the build.
